\r\n
\r\nEven if it's true (which, tbh, is most likely the case), it's\r\nnothing new. Virtually every website uses google analytics these\r\ndays, and that's basically the same - just on a larger scale.
\r\n
\r\nI mean sure, it shouldn't happen, but it doesn't surprise me, and I\r\ndon't see why this huge shitstorm is happening now. It's like all\r\nthese people only now realised that privacy in the surface web is\r\nnot a thing.\\t\\t\\t

\r\nWell thats pretty easy! If someone do not want to be part of BLS\r\nanymore, well okey than, he can leave! Boom Thats It! We go on and\r\ngetting more elitish and special!
\r\n========================================================================
\r\n\r\nSort of. If someone leaves because they want to start their own\r\ngroup or whatever, that's fine. But to leave and then, within\r\nalmost hours, throws hints that they \"May want to come back\", well,\r\nno, because I do not have time for \"wishy-washy\" people..
\r\n
\r\nAnd I say that because, you, of all people, know just how many\r\npeople really want in; want to be here-a waiting list if you will.\r\nAnd I want to be fair to those that have been jumping through our\r\n\"hoops\" and waiting patiently to become part of BLS.
\r\n
\r\nMy word of advise to anyone is to think long and hard before you\r\nclick on the \"leave group\" button, because there will be no turning\r\nback.
\r\n
